[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m243[0m[34m of [0m[33m607[0m[31m ]--[0m
   Rule Id: [34mBD000704[0m
       Tag: [34mSecurity.Backdoor.DataExfiltration.Hostname[0m

   Pattern: [32m.hostname[0m
[30;1m76 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m77 | [0m[35m  In order to not break existing usage, passing a string instead of a tuple to[0m
[30;1m78 | [0m[35m  ``source_address`` will give a DeprecationWarning, and use the value as it if[0m
[30;1m79 | [0m[35m  had been passed for ``local_hostname``.[0m
[30;1m80 | [0m[35m[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m244[0m[34m of [0m[33m607[0m[31m ]--[0m
   Rule Id: [34mBD000704[0m
       Tag: [34mSecurity.Backdoor.DataExfiltration.Hostname[0m
  Severity: [36mImportant[0m, Confidence: [36mLow[0m
  Filename: [33m/aiosmtplib-4.0.0/CHANGELOG.rst[0m
   Pattern: [32m.hostname[0m
[30;1m70 | [0m[35m- **BREAKING**: Remove deprecated ``loop`` keyword argument for the SMTP class.[0m
[30;1m71 | [0m[35m- Change: The ``source_address`` argument now takes a (addr, port) tuple that is[0m
[30;1m72 | [0m[35m  passed as the ``local_addr`` param to ``asyncio.create_connection``, allowing[0m
[30;1m73 | [0m[35m  for binding to a specific IP. The new ``local_hostname`` argument that takes[0m
[30;1m74 | [0m[35m  the value to be sent to the server with the EHLO/HELO message. This behaviour[0m
[30;1m75 | [0m[35m  more closely matches ``smtplib``.[0m
[30;1m76 | [0m[35m[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m245[0m[34m of [0m[33m607[0m[31m ]--[0m
   Rule Id: [34mBD000704[0m
       Tag: [34mSecurity.Backdoor.DataExfiltration.Hostname[0m

   Pattern: [32m.hostname[0m
[30;1m36 | [0m[35m- **BREAKING**: Passing ``source_address`` as a string argument (deprecated in 2.0)[0m
[30;1m37 | [0m[35m  is now an error. ``source_address``  takes a (addr, port) tuple that is used as[0m
[30;1m38 | [0m[35m  the ``local_addr`` param of ``asyncio.create_connection``, allowing for binding[0m
[30;1m39 | [0m[35m  to a specific IP. The ``local_hostname`` argument takes the value to be sent to[0m
[30;1m40 | [0m[35m  the server with the EHLO/HELO message (which is what ``source_address`` was used[0m
[30;1m41 | [0m[35m  for prior to 2.0).[0m
[30;1m42 | [0m[35m- Change: don't use timeout value passed to ``connect`` everywhere,[0m
